USE MASTER 
GO

IF DB_ID('BD_VENTAS') IS NOT NULL	
	DROP DATABASE BD_VENTAS
GO

CREATE DATABASE BD_VENTAS
GO

USE BD_VENTAS
GO

SET DATEFORMAT DMY
GO

CREATE TABLE DISTRITO(
 IDE_DIS INT	NOT NULL IDENTITY(1,1),
 NOM_DIS VARCHAR(50)
)
GO

ALTER TABLE DISTRITO ADD PRIMARY KEY(IDE_DIS)
GO

CREATE TABLE VENDEDOR(
 IDE_VEN INT			NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1,1),
 NOM_VEN VARCHAR(20)	NOT NULL,
 APE_VEN VARCHAR(20)	NOT NULL,
 SUE_VEN MONEY			NOT NULL,
 FEC_ING DATE 			NOT NULL, 
 IDE_DIS INT			NOT NULL
)
GO
 
ALTER TABLE VENDEDOR ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_DIS) REFERENCES DISTRITO(IDE_DIS)
GO

CREATE TABLE CLIENTE(
 IDE_CLI INT			NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1,1),
 RSO_CLI VARCHAR(100)	NOT NULL,
 DIR_CLI VARCHAR(100)	NOT NULL,
 TLF_CLI VARCHAR(15)	NOT NULL,
 RUC_CLI CHAR(11)		NULL,
 IDE_DIS INT			NOT NULL,
 FEC_REG DATE			NOT NULL,
 CON_CLI VARCHAR(50)	NOT NULL
)
GO

ALTER TABLE CLIENTE ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_DIS) REFERENCES DISTRITO(IDE_DIS)
GO

CREATE TABLE PROVEEDOR(
 IDE_PRV INT	NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1,1),
 RAZ_SOC_PRV VARCHAR(80)NOT NULL,
 DIR_PRV VARCHAR(100)NOT NULL,
 TEL_PRV VARCHAR(15) NULL,
 IDE_DIS INT	NOT NULL,
 REP_VEN VARCHAR(80) NOT NULL
)
GO

ALTER TABLE PROVEEDOR ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_DIS) REFERENCES DISTRITO(IDE_DIS)
GO

CREATE TABLE FACTURA(
 NUM_FAC INT	NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1,1),
 FEC_FAC DATE	NOT NULL,
 IDE_CLI INT	NOT NULL,
 FEC_CAN DATE	NOT NULL,
 IDE_VEN INT	NOT NULL
)
GO

ALTER TABLE FACTURA ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_CLI) REFERENCES CLIENTE(IDE_CLI)
ALTER TABLE FACTURA ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_VEN) REFERENCES VENDEDOR(IDE_VEN)

CREATE TABLE ORDEN_COMPRA(
 NUM_OCO INT	NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1,1),
 FEC_OCO DATE	NOT NULL,
 IDE_PRV INT	NOT NULL,
 FEC_ATE DATE	NOT NULL
)
GO

ALTER TABLE ORDEN_COMPRA ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_PRV) REFERENCES PROVEEDOR(IDE_PRV)

CREATE TABLE PRODUCTO(
 IDE_PRO INT	NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1,1),
 DES_PRO  VARCHAR(50)	NOT NULL,
 PRE_PRO MONEY	 NOT NULL,
 SAC_PRO INT NOT NULL,
 SMI_PRO INT NOT NULL,
 UNI_PRO VARCHAR(30)NOT NULL
)
GO

CREATE TABLE DETALLE_FACTURA(
 NUM_FAC INT	NOT NULL,
 IDE_PRO INT	NOT NULL,
 CAN_VEN INT NOT NULL, 
 PRE_VEN MONEY NOT NULL,
 PRIMARY KEY (NUM_FAC,IDE_PRO)
)
GO

ALTER TABLE DETALLE_FACTURA ADD FOREIGN KEY (NUM_FAC) REFERENCES FACTURA(NUM_FAC)
ALTER TABLE DETALLE_FACTURA ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_PRO) REFERENCES PRODUCTO(IDE_PRO)

CREATE TABLE DETALLE_COMPRA(
 NUM_OCO INT	NOT NULL,
 IDE_PRO INT	NOT NULL,
 CAN_PED INT	NOT NULL,
 PRIMARY KEY (NUM_OCO,IDE_PRO)
)
GO

ALTER TABLE DETALLE_COMPRA ADD FOREIGN KEY (NUM_OCO) REFERENCES ORDEN_COMPRA(NUM_OCO)
ALTER TABLE DETALLE_COMPRA ADD FOREIGN KEY (IDE_PRO) REFERENCES PRODUCTO(IDE_PRO)

CREATE TABLE ABASTECIMIENTO(
 IDE_PRV INT	NOT NULL  REFERENCES PROVEEDOR,
 IDE_PRO INT	NOT NULL  REFERENCES PRODUCTO,
 PRE_ABA MONEY  NOT NULL,
 PRIMARY KEY (IDE_PRV,IDE_PRO)
)
GO
